  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_67e13f3c-706d-4943-81fb-7ee9c5566167'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText23095970451370274" style="display:none"><b>Katherine Hart</b> is thrilled to be recruited by Knight Enterprises, the most prestigious venture-capital company in the world. That is, until she makes the acquaintance of the company’s infamous CEO, <b>Dominic Knight</b>.<br /><br />At thirty-two, Dominic is a self-made billionaire with a fearsome ambition and a temper to match. He is also impossibly attractive and dangerously charming when he wants to be.<br /><br />To Kate, Dominic seems like the perfect predator, and she resolves to be cautious despite the obvious chemistry between them, telling herself she can always leave if Dominic grows too demanding. What she doesn’t know is that the decision isn’t hers to make…<br /><br />Dominic Knight has found a new plaything, and Mr. Knight always gets what he wants.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10104242646168464850"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GibbsAllorNothing1USTitlebySueBee_zps2e9a9073.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401846i/780471.jpg' alt=' photo GibbsAllorNothing1USTitlebySueBee_zps2e9a9073.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/GIFDominicKnightbySueBeeUS1_zpsf06b09c3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401846ra/780472.gif' alt=' photo GIFDominicKnightbySueBeeUS1_zpsf06b09c3.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★★! All or Nothing (book 1). The beginning of Nick and Kate’s epic, captivating & addictive story filled with intrigue, suspense, challenges, mind-blowing sex and their intense against-all-odds love!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He shouldn’t even be thinking about dragging her into his wayward world of carnal games. He should give her a free pass. Or maybe just give her the illusion of a free pass. Cold-blooded manipulation or decency? What would it be?”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/>This is the <b>intense whirlwind romanc</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10104242646168464850" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GibbsAllorNothing1USTitlebySueBee_zps2e9a9073.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401846i/780471.jpg" alt=" photo GibbsAllorNothing1USTitlebySueBee_zps2e9a9073.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/GIFDominicKnightbySueBeeUS1_zpsf06b09c3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401846ra/780472.gif" alt=" photo GIFDominicKnightbySueBeeUS1_zpsf06b09c3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! All or Nothing (book 1). The beginning of Nick and Kate’s epic, captivating &amp; addictive story filled with intrigue, suspense, challenges, mind-blowing sex and their intense against-all-odds love!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He shouldn’t even be thinking about dragging her into his wayward world of carnal games. He should give her a free pass. Or maybe just give her the illusion of a free pass. Cold-blooded manipulation or decency? What would it be?”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>This is the <b>intense whirlwind romance</b> between Billionaire Venture Capitalist and CEO of Knight Enterprises, <b>Dominic Knight, Nick</b> and forensic accountant <b>Katherine Hart, Kate.</b> Travel the world over as Nick and Kate’s love develops and is challenged. There will be many twists and turns along the way <b>delivering the very best of intrigue, suspense, sizzling sex and a captivating love</b>. <br><br><u>The All or Nothing Trilogy is using <b>different Publishers</b> for the US and the UK, hence the different covers and titles. Books must be read in order:</u><br>BOOK 1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484196428" rel="nofollow noopener"><b>Knight’s Mistress</b> (UK)</a> / <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484455587" rel="nofollow noopener"><b>All He Wants</b> (US)</a><br>BOOK 2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/530735244" rel="nofollow noopener"><b>Knight’s Game</b> (UK) / <b>All He Needs</b> (US)</a><br>BOOK 3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637496089" rel="nofollow noopener"><b>Knight Takes Queen</b> (UK) / <b>All He Desires</b> (US)</a><br><br><i>
  <b>Nick and Kate almost did not happen!</b>
</i> I say that based on <b>Knight’s Mistress’ (book 1)</b> opening. Magna cum laude graduate of MIT <b>Kate has been flown in by Knight Enterprises to interview for a position of forensic accountant. But their first meeting does not go smoothly</b> as Kate overhears Nick on the phone being strong and demanding. It triggers something in her where she decides to walk away. <br><br>What a way to get Nick’s attention! <b>Not only is he challenged and more determined than ever to employ her, but she has also sparked his interest.</b> Nick, who didn’t even know her name and at the risk of sounding harsh is way out of her league on so many levels, finds himself intrigued and so their story begins... <br><br><b>Follow them to Amsterdam and beyond as Kate works to uncover traitorous threats, both financial and to the reputation of Knight Enterprises.</b> Yet the biggest threat will be to her own heart. <br><br><b>
  <i>Nick is as jaded as they come, getting his attention is one thing, keeping his interest is a whole other story!</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/DGbysb_zps6193ab89.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431825ra/866779.gif" alt=" photo DGbysb_zps6193ab89.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GibbsAllorNothing1-2HerobySueBee_zps64bcc6c1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401846i/780473.jpg" alt=" photo GibbsAllorNothing1-2HerobySueBee_zps64bcc6c1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Dominic Knight, “Nick”</b> is one of those heroes who doesn’t fall in love, rarely even in lust. For him it’s a game. Think of him as a master manipulator - a skilled chess player who has other people do his bidding. <br><br>And… <b>he is my ultimate hero!</b> His combination of <b>uncanny good looks, kinky, devious lover and with his larger-than life, enigmatic, elusive; intense, in-control; ruthless and unyielding personality</b> makes him unforgettable. But what really got me is that he has a <b>maturity and worldliness about him that is unsurpassed</b>! He has staffed homes and fuck-pads in cities across the world. He is the alpha male of alpha males!<br><br>Seven words to describe <b>Nick: Worldly, unforgettable, intense, ruthless, enigmatic, domineering and captivating.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“And what was left behind was an unblinking enigma of a man, ruthless, without borderlines, slippery as mist, beautiful, passionate, remote. And totally and irredeemably loveable.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20heroine/blakelysmilebysb_zpsbe26229c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385368029ra/7134292.gif" alt=" photo blakelysmilebysb_zpsbe26229c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GibbsAllorNothing1-2HeroinebySueBee_zps1a337a06.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401846i/780474.jpg" alt=" photo GibbsAllorNothing1-2HeroinebySueBee_zps1a337a06.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Katherine Hart, “Kate”</b> is smart, even geeky and mostly described as “cute”. I might have wished her more beautiful – even striking (sorry!) and little less moody/confrontational. On the other hand she probably needed to be all that to <b>illustrate the lengths that Dominic will go to appease her even though in all his life he has never bent for anyone</b>. I laughed to myself on numerous occasions when a perplexed Dominic tried to justify his behavior to himself - priceless!<br><br>Five words to describe <b>Kate: Independent, smart, confrontational, moody, endearing and tenacious.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You’re the kind of man who might leave scars,’ she said a moment later, her voice deliberate as though clarifying her position not just to him but to herself.<br>‘But you’re also the kind of man who might end up leaving a tattoo on my sex life that I’ll enjoy looking at later.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Even this third time around <b>Knight’s Mistress’ ending is so shocking I am numb.</b> Nick is everything I could ever ask and hope for in an alpha male hero. He delivers what most strive for, but few succeed at. I don’t know if I’d even call it a cliff-hanger… What I do know is that I will be picking up <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/530735244" rel="nofollow noopener">Book 2</a>, the continuation of their saga! <b>
  <i>Thanks also to my fellow buddy-readers!</i>
</b><br><br><b> Spectacular! Epic! Mesmerizing! Captivating!</b> Nick Knight, the best of the best and unforgettable! <b> 6-star shelf! Thanks Ms. Johnson/Gibbs!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You’ll forget me an hour after I’m gone and I’ll remember you for the rest of my life.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 6 stars <br>Heroine rating: 3.5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5+ stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5+ stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5+ stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes!!!<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes!!!<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/Mogul2bySueBee_zpsd8541242.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385331823ra/7126998.gif" alt=" photo Mogul2bySueBee_zpsd8541242.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>My sincerest thanks to everyone who participated in our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1850399-epic-worldwide-buddy-read-of-all-or-nothing-book-1-on-june-11th" rel="nofollow noopener"><b> Epic worldwide buddy-read</b></a> on CCGibbsFANS!</b><br><br><br><b>Thanks</b> to all the girls on Shh… for our (F) BR on <b>
  <a href="https://goo.gl/0KJcTJ" rel="nofollow noopener">Shh… TopPick</a>
</b><br><br><br>Be sure to <b>join CCGibbsFANS</b> here on GR for the latest news:<br><b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/128147-ccgibbsfans">https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/...</a></b><br><i>(Public group for members 18 years and older)</i></span>

</a><br><br><b>Katherine Hart, “Kate”</b> is smart, even geeky and mostly described as “cute”. I might have wished her more beautiful – even striking (sorry!) and little less moody/confrontational. On the other hand she probably needed to be all that to <b>illustrate the lengths that Dominic will go to appease her even though in all his life he has never bent for anyone</b>. I laughed to myself on numerous occasions when a perplexed Dominic tried to justify his behavior to himself - priceless!<br><br>Five words to describe <b>Kate: Independent, smart, confrontational, moody, endearing and tenacious.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You’re the kind of man who might leave scars,’ she said a moment later, her voice deliberate as though clarifying her position not just to him but to herself.<br>‘But you’re also the kind of man who might end up leaving a tattoo on my sex life that I’ll enjoy looking at later.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Even this third time around <b>Knight’s Mistress’ ending is so shocking I am numb.</b> Nick is everything I could ever ask and hope for in an alpha male hero. He delivers what most strive for, but few succeed at. I don’t know if I’d even call it a cliff-hanger… What I do know is that I will be picking up <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/530735244" rel="nofollow noopener">Book 2</a>, the continuation of their saga! <b>
  <i>Thanks also to my fellow buddy-readers!</i>
</b><br><br><b> Spectacular! Epic! Mesmerizing! Captivating!</b> Nick Knight, the best of the best and unforgettable! <b> 6-star shelf! Thanks Ms. Johnson/Gibbs!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You’ll forget me an hour after I’m gone and I’ll remember you for the rest of my life.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 6 stars <br>Heroine rating: 3.5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5+ stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5+ stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5+ stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes!!!<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes!!!<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/Mogul2bySueBee_zpsd8541242.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385331823ra/7126998.gif" alt=" photo Mogul2bySueBee_zpsd8541242.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>My sincerest thanks to everyone who participated in our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1850399-epic-worldwide-buddy-read-of-all-or-nothing-book-1-on-june-11th" rel="nofollow noopener"><b> Epic worldwide buddy-read</b></a> on CCGibbsFANS!</b><br><br>Be sure to <b>join CCGibbsFANS</b> here on GR for the latest news:<br><b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/128147-ccgibbsfans">https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/...</a></b><br><i>(Public group for members 18 years and older)</i></span>

<div id="review_660193849" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/660193849" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/660193849?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to • Lisa • by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer660193849" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3770639774040654581"><b>4.5 DOMINIC KNIGHT STARS.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385597193i/7182171._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='550' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Readers, if a dominating hero and feisty heroine is what you are looking for then stop the search, drop everything and immerse yourself into the world of Dominic Knight, I guarantee that disappointment will not be making an appearance. Welcome to 'Knights Mistress' a story of lust with no boundaries and love that is not yet realised.<br/><br/><b>What's it all about?</b><br/>Katherine 'Kate' Hart is on the road to success, her hard work, determination and intellect all have led her to this poi</span>
  <span id="freeText3770639774040654581" style="display:none"><b>4.5 DOMINIC KNIGHT STARS.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385597193i/7182171._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Readers, if a dominating hero and feisty heroine is what you are looking for then stop the search, drop everything and immerse yourself into the world of Dominic Knight, I guarantee that disappointment will not be making an appearance. Welcome to 'Knights Mistress' a story of lust with no boundaries and love that is not yet realised.<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>Katherine 'Kate' Hart is on the road to success, her hard work, determination and intellect all have led her to this point; an interview with the self made, infamous billionaire, Dominic knight. Impossibly arrogant and dangerously delicious this CEO always gets what he wants, he never fails and he will go to any length to make sure he succeeds in all that he pursues. So when Kate the feisty redhead attempts to resist the charms of this predator, a game of lust and unstoppable attraction ensues. Question is who will end up winning? And in the end what will they both lose? Find out in this explosive part one of the 'All or nothing' series prepare to fall dangerously in lust.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385328640i/7126699._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385332999i/7127140._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>I enjoyed the unpredictability of this love story, I found myself compelled by their ongoing attraction and lust. This story is a complete page turner every interaction and scene is entertaining and held my interest. The love scenes are poetically erotic, I don't think I've ever been so turned on and at the same time equally impressed by an authors erotic ambition as I have with CC Gibbs. This author has a flair for the extraordinary and there is no doubt that she is able to weave a story that pulled at my interest and had me hanging onto each chapter in anticipation for what would unfold next. The characters are interesting and complex, there is much to learn about both Dominic and Kate. The author has left it wide open for character development, with that in mind I'm hoping to see more storyline and getting to know the characters more in the next two books. As for what I already know, I love Katherine her character is steadfast, womanly, headstrong and intelligent. Her character was introduced brilliantly as an expert in her field and I more than appreciated a female character that could add more to the story line than just her beauty. Dominic Knight is the best kind of fictional character, a little bit damaged, dark and mysterious. CC Gibbs has set up the scene nicely for her readers to be anxiously waiting for more development from this seemingly emotionally void heartthrob. Admittedly there are some similar themes running through this book to other books in this genre but the author has taken it up a level, the writing is beautiful, the story line gripping and the characters are interesting; I couldn't really have asked for much more. Those that like their erotica and intimate scenes to play a starring role in their books I doubt will be disappointed here, although explicitly sensual the writing is engaging and enthralling and the author takes a 'could be over the top' scene and makes it genuinely intimate. Ultimately there will be readers who don't connect with the style of the book or use of another dominant CEO stereotype but I thoroughly enjoyed this romance story with a twist of kink.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385334393i/7127370._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Why not five?</b><br>This start of a trilogy had a five star feeling right up until the 70% mark then I started to loose a little interest and it comes down to one little word - sex, yes as much as I loved this books steamy, erotic chapters there came a point when the book lost some story line and become repetitively steamy, but as far as complaints go it was only a small niggle and overall the book was impressive as well as enjoyable.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385419873i/7145499._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>For those that like their books romantic with a twist of kink you are going to like this impressive book one of a trilogy. Be warned you may want these books lined up to read as a complete series Dominic Knight is ever so wonderfully addictive. So what are you waiting for go grab it readers ... Kisses.<br><br><b>
  <i>*A huge thank you to SueBee for organising the most fabulous buddy read, I loved sharing Dominic with such gorgeous girls ...*</i>
</b></span>

    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1340743810?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781455528325" href="/book/show/17383702-all-he-wants">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-steam-alert">high-steam-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=rich-hottie">rich-hottie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=dominant">dominant</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1340743810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13563507619843408314"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438702600i/15744551.png' width='' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>"Moments mattered in life; they zipped by too fast, or you were looking the other way when you should have been paying attention. Either way you missed them."</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437939826i/15648848.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>When it comes to a modern romance, All He Wants offers a truly cinematic view of pleasure. The combination of descriptive writing and complex characters made this read a sheer delight!<br/><br/>Kate is a highly educated young professional. She has been recruited by Knight Enterprises to investigate losses in the company's financials. When Kate meet</span>
  <span id="freeText13563507619843408314" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438702600i/15744551.png" width="" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"Moments mattered in life; they zipped by too fast, or you were looking the other way when you should have been paying attention. Either way you missed them."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437939826i/15648848.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When it comes to a modern romance, All He Wants offers a truly cinematic view of pleasure. The combination of descriptive writing and complex characters made this read a sheer delight!<br><br>Kate is a highly educated young professional. She has been recruited by Knight Enterprises to investigate losses in the company's financials. When Kate meets Dominic Knight, she is instantly put on alert by his domineering personality and kurt speech. Despite her reservations in accepting the job, she concedes and she takes off for Amsterdam in order to complete the work. <br><br> <b>"Dominic Knight in all his dark, sensual beauty was standing there, up close and personal, his quick raking glance so casually assessing she should take offense, not feel a shocking rush of pleasure."-Kate</b><br><br>Dominic is a womanizer. After the passing of his wife, he has found pleasure in anything that he wants. He is taken by Kate but only because she represents innocence that he is desperate to taint and tantalize! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437939826i/15648849.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Dominic doesn't waste any time trying to seduce his young employee. After much uncertainty, Kate agrees to a relationship with Mr. Knight of JUST SEX for a few days. The two share and experience some highly charged moments of sexual pleasure together. <br><br><b>"This holiday was about sex and games of mastery and submission, power and control. Nothing else."-Dominic</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437939932i/15648863.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> They explore Amsterdam, Shanghai, and Hong Kong together. As in most cases when sexual chemistry is evident, these two begin to develop feelings for one another. Kate is terrified of getting her heart broken. Dominic has spent so many years keeping himself guarded from love and yet, Kate begins to spark a deep feeling of longing deep in his soul.<br><br>As the clock is ticking, I felt more and more love for these characters. Of course, I will have to continue the series to see what happens next.<br><br><b>"He was the only man she'd ever wanted, perhaps the only man she'd ever want. How would she survive without him?"-Kate</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437939826i/15648850.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> <b>"It was like reaching home after an endless journey. Or finding safe haven from a storm. Or perhaps, finding love for those with an open mind."-Dominic</b><br><br>Overall, All He Wants was a very good read. At first, I found myself very frustrated with Kate. She was so uncertain about herself and what choices she should make. I thoroughly enjoyed observing the transformation that takes place in her as the story progressed. Dominic is no doubt a typical "alpha male" who is taken down a notch or two when Kate dishes out some highly charged verbal banter. I can honestly say once the book took off, I couldn't put it down. I did find the POV in the text to be a bit confusing at times. It shifts rather abruptly and if was slightly problematic to sift through especially during highly charged moments in the story. The sexual encounters between Kate and Dominic were off the charts! Ms. Gibbs is quite gifted at evoking every drop of emotion and sexual tension from these two. However, what makes this read so remarkable is the authors ability to paint the settings so vividly. Her descriptions of each location made me feel like I was on vacation enjoying the sights, smells, and sounds right along with the main characters. That, my friends, made this read a true winner for me! I highly recommend this book to anyone that enjoys a modern romance that is staged in stunning locations. Although this was a slow starter for me, once the conflict was in place, I couldn't stop reading! I will certainly be following up with Kate and Dominic in the next installment of this series.<br><br><b>~BR with my girls at SHH! In preparation for an upcoming Indie Star Chat!~</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436073301r/15415875.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> <b>~ARC graciously offered by author in exchange for an honest review. Thank you Ms. Gibbs for sharing your work with me.~</b><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://craziesrusbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/667200759?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam" href="/user/show/13865261-pam">Pam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18165746-all-he-wants">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

This was erotica at it's best, with so much foreplay and heat burning through almost every page. This game they played was a dangerous one, riding the line between lust and hate, but nothing, I mean NOTHING prepared them for the <i>need, the craving and the longing</i> that they had for one another. They loved to fight, mad and themselves and took it out on each other, fucking the fight out of them. <br><br>Dominic is a man who can have anything he wants, used to being able to control everything and anything around him for the right price. He has the world in his disposal and isn't ashamed to call on it when he needs to. He never tried to downplay his power, he simply forced it down anyone's throat and made everyone accept it. Everyone always wants something from him, feeding his arrogance...until Kate. She took his high and mighty self down a couple notches, and even still the Dominic he is with her is still unbearable with his need for control. Kate is a ball-breaker, and after she has given Dominic a piece of her mind, she succumbs to all that is him; loving the way he makes her feel and hating herself for being so weak. <br><br>I highly enjoyed Dominic and Kate's beginning, as crazy as it was, I couldn't put the book down. I had to continue on and see it through, caught up in the lavish life that he lives and all the pleasures he has mastered to share. The sex was OTT, nothing in a kinky way but just excessive than the norm. But what I realized is that, that is what makes Dominic and Kate... it was their way of proving to us and to each other the extent of their need and craving for one another. <br><br>There is no major outside drama, no straying regardless of his past, the story is really about them and how they are both coping with their new found feelings. They contradicted themselves getting lost in the moment, but they fight themselves as much as they fight each other. This dual POV is a crazy-sexy-whirlwind romance that is worth the read for all my erotica friends!<br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485762577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13533463114876005712">I have to say that I think the blurb is little misleading and it makes Dominic out to be some kind of sexual predator who will have Kate whatever her reservations because he’s made up his mind but Dominic is a much more moral character than he is described there and actually fights his attraction to Kate for a long time.<br/><br/>It took me a while to get into this one but when I did it was worth it. It’s got a different feel to a lot of the erotic trilogies out there – these two sparred verbally, back an</span>
  <span id="freeText13533463114876005712" style="display:none">I have to say that I think the blurb is little misleading and it makes Dominic out to be some kind of sexual predator who will have Kate whatever her reservations because he’s made up his mind but Dominic is a much more moral character than he is described there and actually fights his attraction to Kate for a long time.<br /><br />It took me a while to get into this one but when I did it was worth it. It’s got a different feel to a lot of the erotic trilogies out there – these two sparred verbally, back and forth, for at least the first third of the book, intellectually challenging one another. They’re incredibly verbose as they launch their acerbic wit at one another like ballistic missiles. For a while, I felt like I was on the outside looking in, not entirely immersed in their story but, eventually, as Kate finally succumbed to the intense burning desire she has for Dominic I became drawn in and thoroughly enjoyed it.<br /><br />We don’t suddenly go straight into strong D/s. It all starts off as vanilla, really rather intense vanilla, but vanilla all the same but Knight is absolutely a dominant and his control comes to the fore pretty quickly and it’s not long before he’s controlling their sex life and it’s pretty intensely erotic. Definitely gets the juices flowing that’s for sure!! They are overwhelmed by their passion for one another, their mutual attractions is positively incendiary, they are both highly-sexed and just cannot keep their hands off one another.<br /><br />Despite the whole jet-set billionaire storyline, the development of the relationship felt very believable. The constant verbal sparring which, at first, distanced me from the story worked well in helping me to get to know the characters and I sunk deeper and deeper into their growing relationship until I was drowning in it and just didn’t want to come up for air.<br /><br />Kate is a totally beguiling heroine – she’s open, engaging, unfailingly honest. There’s a lot to admire in her and she’s not about to roll over like a doormat and totally submit to Dominic. She never makes things easy for him and he’s completely off his game when she’s around. She’s very distracting to him and suddenly, everything he’s worked so hard for, is starting to seem less important much to the distaste of those closest to him.<br /><br />Knight is not your typical fictional brooding billionaire. He’s open, garrulous, tender and caring. He wants to dominate Kate right from the start but he knows that he needs to bide his time, tread on eggshells and slowly woo her until she’s a hot wet mess for him and can no longer resisit.<br /><br />He did a few things that I didn’t like including taking control of Kate’s birth control pills and threatening not to give her them back.<br /><br />As I slowly approached the ending, I watched my Kindle Paperwhite count down the reading time remaining in the bottom left hand corner with growing sadness. I really wanted to carry on with them as I knew the ending would leave me twitching with dissatisfaction as this is a trilogy an the story will continue. When I did finally get to the end,it was not without a minor hissy fit as I am now desperate to know what will happen next.<br /><br />Part 2, Knight’s Retreat, is not due for release until June 2013 and I need it – PDQ! CC Gibbs – I have absolutely no idea who you are but you’ve caught me in your spell with the beautiful, elegant writing style and enthralling characters and compelling storyline. This doesn’t feel like a debut – this feels like the work of an established author. I feel a little lost and bereft now that I have finished part 1.<br /><br />4 stars erotic romance<br /><br />Series Reading Order<br /><br />1. Knight's Mistress<br />2. Knight's Retreat - anticipated release date June 2013<br />3. <div id="review_775117207" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/775117207" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/775117207?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer775117207" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12653056260708241184"><br/><b>
  <blockquote>"All because of a slip of a woman with red curls and bright green eyes." </blockquote>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386601693i/7400331.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Knights Mistress had me confused with my feelings, I felt torn by the end.... Did I love it??? Did I love the characters???? It has all the ingredients that make a book epic for me, but something didn't quite connect with my heart, as it should, for an epic read. Almost the whole way through I was not really feeling it, not connecting to the characters, dare I say, I was a little bored, I can see why a few people 'did n</span>
  <span id="freeText12653056260708241184" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <blockquote>"All because of a slip of a woman with red curls and bright green eyes." </blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386601693i/7400331.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Knights Mistress had me confused with my feelings, I felt torn by the end.... Did I love it??? Did I love the characters???? It has all the ingredients that make a book epic for me, but something didn't quite connect with my heart, as it should, for an epic read. Almost the whole way through I was not really feeling it, not connecting to the characters, dare I say, I was a little bored, I can see why a few people 'did not finish'. But... I know some great people on Goodreads and some of those great people adore this series. I knew there had to be a reason, so I carried on regardless. And I have to say, I'm really glad I did.... I think!!!<br><br><i>Let me tell you my thoughts and my wishes....</i><br><br>Our hero is Dominic, a thirty-two year old, self-made billionaire, who is emotionally detached, ambitious, a playboy and hot tempered in and out of the bedroom. His company, Knight Enterprises, is the most prestigious venture-capital company in the world. They need a forensic accountant and<i> Katherine Hart </i>is the girl they want on their team.....<br><br>Kate is intelligent, sassy, opinionated and sexy. She has her very own temper....<br><br>More about Dominic <br><b>"Dominic Knight had an eye for beauty."</b> And his eye is firmly set on our heroine, and what Mr Knight wants.... <i>Mr Knight gets!!!</i> He's an all or nothing kind of guy.<br><br><b>"You don't say no to me..... Nobody says no to me!"</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386663156ra/7417483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"His smile was so sexy it had to be illegal."</b> He's gorgeous, charming, controlling and domineering in the extreme..... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386673300i/7418417._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I want you available for fucking."</b><br><i>He had a proposition for her... Would she take it??? Would that be enough for either of them??? </i><br><br>Dominic and Kate have great banter between them and have an immense Chemistry, I can't say I always felt it, but by the end they had me convinced.<br><br><b>"...impressive; male perfection..."</b><br>He's an expert in all things of a sexual nature!!! And a very good expert given the orgasmic results for Kate.<br><br>The story is an erotic tale,<b>
  <blockquote> "About pragmatism and the sad ache of regret. About love and longing, about the shadow of fear that was so strong it was making her ears buzz. About the rising panic of losing......"</blockquote>
</b> Losing her, losing him, losing your way of life and opening up your heart, sharing your life, body, heart and soul.<i> Sounds beautiful doesn't it?</i> It was beautiful in places and HIGHLY erotic... <b>Oh YES!!!!</b> <br><br><i>
  <b>I wish I loved it more.....</b>
</i><br>I would describe the writing as being third person in the extreme, I felt like I got the inner thoughts of everyone, even a shop assistant, and sometimes that threw me off balance and I think it may have affected my connection with the main characters... <br><br>I found some of the dialogue a bit clunky and unrealistic, in contrast some of it was extremely poetic and lyrical. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386674504i/7418519.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Beautiful</i><br><br>Dominic talks to Kate in a very direct manner about things. It makes his character seem a little monotone.<br><br>The characters blew very hot and cold with their words and actions to the extent it made them feel inconsistent to me.<br><br>I feel like I have a love hate relationship with this story.<br><br>How did I get to 3 stars??? Well....<br>Even though my connection to the characters was slow, I still found my heart breaking at the end for them. I guess you could say this one snuck up on me…??? I didn’t expect to feel as emotionally connected as I did by the end??? <br><br>He’s an all or nothing kind of guy. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386674504i/7418520._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>If you love domineering men and erotic tales you should give this series a try. xoxox<br><br>♥ BR with lots of lovely ladies. <br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12653056260708241184" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6991089608344338237"><b>5 "Knight-Gasmic" Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/DominicKnight_zps666d0499.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

Yes, please</b><br/><br/><b>ALL OR NOTHING</b> series is amply named. <b>Dominic Knight</b> is looking to hire a forensic account to find out who's stealing money from Knight Enterprises. <b>Kate</b> happens to the woman for the job even though she isn't sure she wants to work for Mr. Knight.<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397880769i/9341139._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Dominic is a cold-hearted bastard who gets what he wants every.single.time. When Kate interviewed for the job he knew she was the one. He liked how she challenged him. Kate's no-nonsense attitude keeps Dominic reeling </span>

Yes, please</b><br><br><b>ALL OR NOTHING</b> series is amply named. <b>Dominic Knight</b> is looking to hire a forensic account to find out who's stealing money from Knight Enterprises. <b>Kate</b> happens to the woman for the job even though she isn't sure she wants to work for Mr. Knight.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397880769i/9341139._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Dominic is a cold-hearted bastard who gets what he wants every.single.time. When Kate interviewed for the job he knew she was the one. He liked how she challenged him. Kate's no-nonsense attitude keeps Dominic reeling as he tries to please her.<br><br>Looking forward to finding out where this story takes me.<br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17383702.All_He_Wants__All_Or_Nothing___1_" title="All He Wants (All Or Nothing, #1) by C.C.     <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/952228790?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Beverly by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer952228790" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9871643718706129196"><b>* * * * * 5 All In Stars * * * * *</b><br/><br/><b>Dominic Knight...</b>is the epitome of alpha male. He is demanding, protective, unyielding, and over the top. As owner and CEO of Knight Industries, Dominic is used to getting what he wants. So when <b>Katherine Hart</b>, recent MIT graduate, declines Dominic’s employment offer, he decides to make accommodations to get his way. <br/><br/><b>And the fun begins…</b><br/><br/>Katherine is sent to Amsterdam to solve a finance problem, and Dominic decides to tag along a few days later thus beginning thei</span>
  <span id="freeText9871643718706129196" style="display:none"><b>* * * * * 5 All In Stars * * * * *</b><br /><br /><b>Dominic Knight...</b>is the epitome of alpha male. He is demanding, protective, unyielding, and over the top. As owner and CEO of Knight Industries, Dominic is used to getting what he wants. So when <b>Katherine Hart</b>, recent MIT graduate, declines Dominic’s employment offer, he decides to make accommodations to get his way. <br /><br /><b>And the fun begins…</b><br /><br />Katherine is sent to Amsterdam to solve a finance problem, and Dominic decides to tag along a few days later thus beginning their 8 days around the world. <br /><br />Dominic was perfection to me. I love an alpha asshole and a dirty talker is a cherry on top. He had me gasping at how direct and confident he was, and let me tell you a confident man: SEXY AS HELL!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“...Answer or I’ll take my dick where the women are more accommodating.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Kate knows Dominic is trouble. She is concerned with her career, the way she is perceived, but who can resist Dominic?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>And for the first time, she truly understood the corrupting power of desire—the ache, the need, the wanting that never stopped, the breathless, fatal longing.</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>What I loved…</b><br /><br />Um…Dominic…enough said. I am only kidding. You should read this because this story sweeps you away to world most of us don’t experience everyday or may never experience. Additionally, I loved watching Nick and Kate’s story progress. I had my thoughts as to what would happen, and how things would develop and I was wrong. Of course, I can’t just skim over the steam factor….this book was thru the roof in hotness. Nick..sigh…I can’t even put into words.<br /><br />This is a series and I cannot wait to start book two, to see where my Nick ends up. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>Thank you so much SuzyQ, I loved it!<br /><br /></i>
</b></span>

It's been out in the UK for quite a while under the title Knight's Mistress and as soon as I read the blurb I knew I had to have it..   <span id="freeText10302129250750790427" style="display:none"><i>
  <b> 5 Panty Melting Sexy Billionaire Stars!</b>
</i><br /><br />I'd been waiting for the release of this on in the US for months.. It's been out in the UK for quite a while under the title Knight's Mistress and as soon as I read the blurb I knew I had to have it.. Yes, it's another super rich controlling billionaire book but still can't get enough of them ;). And this one was good... really really good. Very sexy.. the sex was just crazy hot. We do have the typical super rich guy,Dominick, with a wounded past, can't commit to anything but making money, has some naughty sexual vices, is controlling.. bla bla bla.. you know the type. Then we have Kate.. honestly Kate really got on my nerves to begin with. She was at times very strong willed and wouldn't take any shit off Dom, then she'd be melting at his feet at the crook of his finger. But well.. I really couldn't blame her cause that man was talented. She lost conscience one time from so many bit O's in a row. That man is lethal! He's an orgasm ninja! Kate falls quickly for Dom but he's in the same boat.. she's afraid he'll never be able to commit and Dom feels he never will be able to either. That ending just broke my heart.... and yes, its a cliffhanger but it doesn't end crazy.... it was a good place to end. I hope December gets here quickly because I need more Dom and Kate..<br /><br />If sexy billionaires with a need for control are your thing.. then this one is right up your ally.. </span>

</a><br/><br/>When Katherine Hart, newest recruit to Knight Enterprises, meets self assured, dominant and totally sexy, self made millionaire and company CEO; Dominic Knight, the sexual chemistry between the two is clearly evident, but Katherine wants to avoid the man she sees as predator, she doesn't want to be just another one of his conquests. Trouble is, Dominic has other ideas and he's not about to just walk away. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zpsb8d9dacb.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>I really enjoyed this story. The authors writing style was entertaining, descriptiv</span>
  <span id="freeText13831718397641238279" style="display:none"><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zpsed38615c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>When Katherine Hart, newest recruit to Knight Enterprises, meets self assured, dominant and totally sexy, self made millionaire and company CEO; Dominic Knight, the sexual chemistry between the two is clearly evident, but Katherine wants to avoid the man she sees as predator, she doesn't want to be just another one of his conquests. Trouble is, Dominic has other ideas and he's not about to just walk away. <br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zpsb8d9dacb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428020i/855975._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsb8d9dacb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really enjoyed this story. The authors writing style was entertaining, descriptive and totally addictive. It was what I call, a definite page turner. I loved Kate, she was independent, sassy, confident and endearing and not a complete doormat who just laid back and thought of England. She was head strong and not afraid to argue.<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zps31a83f40.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428020i/855976._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps31a83f40.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The story line was erotic and sensual as well as romantic and emotional, it was also believable and not at all predictable. I would loved to have discovered more about Dominic's past but I guess this has been saved for book 2, a book I will definitely be opening up next! <br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zps4077d95f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>Thanks for recommendation Lili and SueBee x</span>

  <span id="freeText11859503917957972204" style="display:none">WARNING: REVIEW MAY CONTAIN PROFANITY OR OTHER ADULT CONTENT. <br /><br /><br /><br />Ok. Slow start, quick finish, breathless end. Just like a good mindfuck should be. <br /><br />SPOILERS TOO!! You have been warned. <br />Don't read any further if you don't want to know. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br />This started off as a real slow burner for me. For a while I even thought I might not finish. <br />Ok so the sexual attraction was there right from the beginning, a tangible, physical draw. She fought it, she knew she was a moth to the flame. Oh she wanted him but could see it would be at an emotional price she couldn't afford. He didn't care; he wanted to fuck her and couldn't imagine that not happening and on whatever terms he chose. <br />She said no to him: twice. WTF. <br />But he knew that at the most primal level she wanted him. So he set about using her own body against her rational reluctance. He stoked her desire and used his unassailable resources to secure her capitulation. <br />Just like a business deal, he made her an offer her body could not refuse. Clinched the deal, to the victor the spoils. <br />But what's he won??? He was so keen to win at all costs he didn't even realise the unconscious concessions he was making.<br />So: he's got his sex toy for a week. But now he's invested so much in her he's lost his focus, lost himself even starts fantasising about playing Russian Roulette with her reproductive organs and gives voice to his madness that he wants to impregnate her. She clearly hears him but, amazingly doesn't freak out and keeps her focus on chasing the next orgasm. In a Damascene moment they both hit the reality button and the birth control dilemma is resolved in favour of swallowing the pill. <br />Fast forward through some intense, white hot, Fuckery and OMG she can't resist the reality. One orgasm too many and it slips out, she has to say the three little words. <br />By now we know he's smitten, right ??? But he can't say that, of course not. He can move mountains and change his world for her though. He starts to: but then he can't do it. His world is too secure in his grasp. <br />She wakes from her last scheduled night of unbridled lust to write him a letter. She can't surrender, can't stay, can't become absorbed by him. <br />Too late. He's already gone. He's trumped her Ace. Elvis has left the building. <br />Jesus Christ. Now we've got to wait until June 2013.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer772607243" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15423348549336554284">4.5 Stars. <br/><br/>Scoot on over Christian and Gideon, there's a new alpha in town! Dominic Knight, 32-year old billionaire CEO of Knight enterprises, may just steal your heart. <br/><br/>Katherine Hart, recent top graduate at MIT, is a specialist in forensic technology. When she is approached by Knight Enterprises to assist in the investigation of shady business in their Amsterdam office, she's very interested. That is, until she meets their CEO. Overhearing him screaming on the phone, throwing out profanities, </span>
  <span id="freeText15423348549336554284" style="display:none">4.5 Stars. <br><br>Scoot on over Christian and Gideon, there's a new alpha in town! Dominic Knight, 32-year old billionaire CEO of Knight enterprises, may just steal your heart. <br><br>Katherine Hart, recent top graduate at MIT, is a specialist in forensic technology. When she is approached by Knight Enterprises to assist in the investigation of shady business in their Amsterdam office, she's very interested. That is, until she meets their CEO. Overhearing him screaming on the phone, throwing out profanities, she quickly decides this is not the job for her. But Knight doesn't take "no" for an answer...ever. Begin the power struggle between these two strong characters. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=10cd52850d41adc67bcf209925dae9c2_zps74616954.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385335148i/7127463._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=8983d31c6f83d1657e3fa9c3147a0fd1_zpsd3d1bfe4.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385335148i/7127464._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kate is hell-bent not to let Mr. Knight control her. He quickly turns from boss to a man that clearly wants a sexual relationship. She pushes back at every turn. She will NOT be yet another notch on this guy's bed post. He may have researched the hell out of her for this position but two can play that game. She knows he's into kink...the videos she's seen! She's as vanilla as they come. <br><br>Knight has everything the world has to offer at his fingertips. He can buy anything, achieve anything, but getting this girl into his bed is one feat he didn't realize would be so challenging. And that just turns him on even more...she's a tough cookie, stands up to all his antics, hell, he wants her even more now. He WILL succeed in bedding Miss Hart.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=1663771c5549562d9ea60092bf910a10_zps3c1a9e39.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385468779i/7155735._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Once this battle of wills cave to temptation, this book is filled with erotic, captivating love scenes. Nick knows she's vanilla but things very gradually turn more D/s. But the banter continues...<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=94a6d279895cbc2cdca5dde3f3b36b97_zps96f62927.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Dominic Knight is the perfect alpha. He's subtly controlling every aspect of Kate's life, unbeknownst to her. He has staff everywhere at his disposal. Everything a carefully planned out game with Miss Hart his conquest. But can he do both...continue his life of a renowned business mogul with holdings all over the world, AND fulfill his every fantasy with this girl who's got him all wrapped up? It may look like he's call ing the shots but she's the one truly in control here. Can he have it all...business and pleasure? We won't call it love. Mr. Knight won't ever admit to love...<br><br>Both characters are super like-able. I instantly attached myself to his character. A widower, it's clear he has secrets making it difficult to attach emotionally to Kate. Ah, Kate, the snarky STRONG, feisty heroine that throws this man off his game like no other woman has. It was a serious game of chess...he'd make her move, she hers. But the game is not over for them...<br><br>Looking forward to the continuing story of Dominic Knight and Katherine Hart. It's sexy, erotic, and captivating. CC Gibbs' writing is poetically eloquent. One scene just completely captivated me from the writing alone...<br><br><b>"Deciding Miss Hart had been suitably gratified, he finally indulged himself. Plunging deeper, he shut his eyes against the sudden, intense, improbable shock of impact and wondered for a moment if he was going to come instantly like some sixteen-year-old fucking for the first time. Christ! Panting, he managed to restrain himself for a moment because he wouldn't allow himself to be so undisciplined. But self-willed or not, he could no longer stop the orgasmic surge building inside him and his climax broke in a teeth-clenched, mind-blowing, seemingly endless seminal flood that filled the lovely Miss Hart. And surely shook his composure." </b><br><br>Have you EVER read an orgasm scene like that? Sweet Jesus that was awesome. The book is riddled with beautifully written prose like that. Looking forward to the next installment of the story of Nick and Kate!<br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/957183827?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer957183827" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3187908348873253702">3.5 STARS<br/><br/>The billionaire bachelor story line is a familiar one, you could also say it's been exhausted. So in order to stand out it has to bring something different to the table. I liked this book, and ultimately it did bring something a little different to a sub-genre overflowing with cliches. <br/>Dominic Knight is a billionaire that oversees everything to his company. He's detailed, ruthless, arrogant and doesn't take no for an answer. Women are distractions, play-things, that fill a void and sati</span>
  <span id="freeText3187908348873253702" style="display:none">3.5 STARS<br /><br />The billionaire bachelor story line is a familiar one, you could also say it's been exhausted. So in order to stand out it has to bring something different to the table. I liked this book, and ultimately it did bring something a little different to a sub-genre overflowing with cliches. <br />Dominic Knight is a billionaire that oversees everything to his company. He's detailed, ruthless, arrogant and doesn't take no for an answer. Women are distractions, play-things, that fill a void and satisfy a need. When Kate Hart interviews for a position as a forensic accountant, Nick never expected her to turn down his offer. But once she does, he makes it his mission to bring her on board...and into his bed.<br /><br />This started out slow for me. The difference between this book and others probably comes down to the intelligence of the story, and the way it's told. 3rd person pov that rotates among not only the main characters but some secondary ones as well, was refreshing. It gave me a better glimpse of how the world viewed Nick and his increasingly obvious infatuation with Kate. The vocabulary here was also much more diverse. The book is well written and the descriptions very detailed. But aside from that, the story didn't pick up for me till around the 60-65% mark. Before that I often had a hard time paying attention. But after that, something changed. The intensity between Nick and Kate increased exponentially. What started out as playful banter and lustful interaction became much more, things became MORE. More serious, more romantic, more AT STAKE. Walking away became unthinkable, excruciating, painful.<br /><br />That's what I think changed everything for me. Nick was often justifying his thoughts, feelings, desires for Kate. It was amusing to watch him deny anything resembling love or romance. But to the reader it was so obvious! <br />I did like Nick, he was really hot! By the end I loved him. He was so generous, giving, sweet, thoughtful, accommodating. The man got to the point thathe was willing to lose billions, put his company in jeopardy, just to be with Kate. WOW. I actually felt his turmoil, his constant battle within himself. He really turned the book around for me.<br />I started out okay with Kate, then I didn't like her for the majority of the book. She was argumentative, difficult and childish at times. Granted, she was 22, but she pissed me off. But slowly I understood why she was that way. Nick is intimidating. His past daunting for anyone, let alone a young and inexperienced girl from the Midwest. It became clear that Kate was overloading on defense mechanisms. By the end, I really liked her, and I only hope I stay liking her as I continue with the series.<br /><br />The ending was not a cliffy per se, more like a To Be Continued. But I felt the urgent need to one click the second book right away. Kate's reaction to<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Nick up and leaving her without a word <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>killed me. I was so upset. She seemed alright with everything but she's excellent at defending herself. I want to see Nick<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[regret his decision and grovel to get her back, even if she wanted to leave <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br /><br />I also want to say thanks to all the fabulous buddy readers! Thank you SueBee and Nicole for letting me know about this epic read! It's a beautiful thing to know that no matter where you live in the world, you can always connect with fellow lovers of literature! <br /><br /><br />CCGibbsFans epic buddy read, rejoice! </span>
  <a data-text-id="3187908348873253702" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText15880961426334076847" style="display:none"><b>5 All Knight Long Stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390885840i/8294935.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Kate Hart is fresh out of MIT and is in high demand. But Dominic is not going to take no for an answer. <br><br>Kate agrees to come on board as a contracted consultant, a job that has an expiration date. As she begins to unravel the cyber theft of funds from Knight Enterprises, Dominic is ensuring that their paths will cross again.<br><br>Dominic is not a man of simple tastes, he prefers his women submissive and at times, paid for. He’s not the kind of man that turns down an opportunity. But he is far beyond Kate’s sexual experience. His tastes aren’t a secret, it only takes a quick search to find that Dominic prefers a bit of a bite to his sex. But even knowing that, Kate can’t seem to say no to him.<br><br>So begins the affair. With a limited amount of days left with her in his employment and under his thumb, Dominic plans on taking every advantage of Miss Hart. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390885840i/8294936.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>This was one explosive read. <span id="freeTextContainer12295026919305221654"><i>Written June 19, 2014</i><br/><br/><b>3.7 Stars - A charming Billionaire Bad Boy romance - Boiling hot and well done. <br/><br/>Book #1</b><br/><br/>I've had this novel <i>Knight's Mistress</i> lying here in a, by know pretty dusty, paperback since last summer. A friend recommended it and when I heard that the same sweet <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6578577.C_C__Gibbs' title='C.C. Gibbs' rel='nofollow noopener'>C.C. Gibbs</a>-loving friend, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user_status/show/44623478' rel='nofollow noopener'>SueBee</a>, organized a <i>"Epic worldwide buddy-read of 'All or Nothing', book 1"</i> I felt it was my great chance to at last read this book, so I joined. <br/><br/><a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
