</a><a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>A rich hunk always gets a beautif</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12295026919305221654" style="display:none"><i>Written June 19, 2014</i><br><br><b>3.7 Stars - A charming Billionaire Bad Boy romance - Boiling hot and well done. <br><br>Book #1</b><br><br>I've had this novel <i>Knight's Mistress</i> lying here in a, by know pretty dusty, paperback since last summer. A friend recommended it and when I heard that the same sweet <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6578577.C_C__Gibbs" title="C.C. Gibbs" rel="nofollow noopener">C.C. Gibbs</a>-loving friend, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user_status/show/44623478" rel="nofollow noopener">SueBee</a>, organized a <i>"Epic worldwide buddy-read of 'All or Nothing', book 1"</i> I felt it was my great chance to at last read this book, so I joined. <br><br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>A rich hunk always gets a beautiful young woman to get caught on the hook, but he've to struggle a bit.</b><br><i>Knight's Mistress</i> is the first part in a three book series in the "billionaire bad boy erotic romance genre". I have to admit that I'm pouting a bit over the end of this first book, but a three part story IS a three part story. Not a horrible and terrible cliff hanger, but still. ~ Otherwise, was this novel well written, quite fun and insanely steamy. <br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><b>Katherine Hart</b> is high and thrilled for the chance to get her first job ever at <i>Knight Enterprises</i>, the most prestigious venture-capital company in the world. She is a newbie with a just finished education at the university and becomes giddily surprised when she gets a very good offer for a job at the company's <i>Amsterdam</i> office. The offer is also individually from the company’s <b>infamous CEO, Dominic Knight</b>. <br><br>...But that man is more than her well-being can handle so she thanks definite no. Dominic know, however, how someone can be persuaded, and a few hours later, Kate sits on a flight to Europe.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/albums/w615/Li64/City%20and%20nature%20etc/?action=view&amp;current=bd3a9704d1ebe004ba452f428befa8d2_zps9a6400ef.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402600162i/9958675.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <br>
  <i>It all start in beautiful Amsterdam...</i>
</blockquote><br>So suddenly appears (anyone surprised?) the "Man of the Men", Dominic Knight in Amsterdam and everything starts rolling at a fast, burning hot, pace. <b>Jeez, this slightly kinky man knows how to get a woman</b> to where he wants her. There are beautiful clothes, sexy innuendos and very seductive words. <br><br>Just some day later their now heated erotic adventure flying on to the beautiful Asian metropolis, <i>Singapore</i>...<br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/albums/w615/Li64/City%20and%20nature%20etc/?action=view&amp;current=fe9cee15776b503e9f208143ee3b7a8c_zpsfec661d7.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402784715i/9986525.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“You’re the kind of man who might leave scars,” she said a moment later, her voice deliberate as though clarifying her position not just to him but to herself. <br>“But you’re also the kind of man who might end up leaving a tattoo on my sex life that I’ll enjoy looking at later.” </blockquote><br>...to just a few days later at last land in <i>Hong Kong</i>. A place Dominic maybe should call his 'home' and where his great big mansion (and also the small secret...) and a lot of friends (including his bitchy mother) and observe staff are.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/albums/w615/Li64/City%20and%20nature%20etc/?action=view&amp;current=434e1551c6a01e08af4b8a17c2203f63_zps2ee0ef12.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403185641i/10054714.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><b>And it is here in Hong Kong their bedroom-play</b>, and maybe also future love-story, starts for real.<br><blockquote>“I want you to understand who’s in charge of your climax the next few days,” he coolly said. “So there’s no misunderstandings.” </blockquote><br>***********************************************************<br><br>It was a lot of fun to read an m/f romance in this steamy "billionaire bad boy" genre again. It was a long time since last...<br><br># <b>He, Dominic is a man on the highest top</b>. A charming man who always dominate a room. He is larger, sexier, younger, stronger, tougher, more handsome and just a rich dream alpha. (...a "larger-than-life hero" as SueBee says)<br># <b>She, Kate is a intelligent small town girl</b> without much experience. She has a simpler and more straightforward way, is less showy, curvier (he likes big boobs..) and more natural than the women he usually takes for the night.<br><br>I liked these two characters. Perhaps they are stereotypes in this as in many romances —rich older man and poor young girl— but I still think the heroine was independent enough and the hero was humorous fun and not just a horny caveman with a rich man's features.<br><blockquote>‘Innocence waiting to be fucked, he pleasantly thought. And his, he decided with the proprietary instincts of a modern princeling.’</blockquote><br><b>Sometimes I felt it was a pity that the author made Kate so young</b> (23). Most often, feels and performs she anyway as a much older woman. I haven't read so many romances in this contemporary billioners genre, but I really think Kate is outstanding mature and she haven't fallen into that usual damsel in distress boring "drool-for-the-alpha-hero" trap. I hope she'll continue to stand up for herself in the next two books. <br><br>~ I kind of like, and smiles, when Dominic had to act as a better man and bend his knees. <br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/albums/w615/Li64/Couple%20in%20love/?action=view&amp;current=image_zpsd96e1bff.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403186827i/10054865.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br>***********************************************************<br><br>But, there are (course...) some few <u>but's</u> from me. - As when Kate really is like a cute cuddly kitten. She <i>purrs</i> enormously, over again and over again, at Dominic's command. And I can't but wonder; How many times is it possible? Within half an hour? <br><br><b>I know this is a fairy tale romance with high ambition in the erotic part</b>. But after all, sometimes would actually a little less, rather than a lot, increase the credibility and sense of what is happening. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I know he's very skilled, experienced, well-equipped and talented with his hands and his hearty own <i>weapon</i> in the bedroom. It need not be proved again and again. I by know also now that he additionally can give a woman (as this young inexperienced Kate) almost world record in number of female <i>pleasures</i>. ~ Really? Twice a day?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><b>Kinky and D/s playing?</b><br>As always was I a bit afraid to see that (scary) whip, other 'sex-toys' and to much tough Dom action. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I'm not a big fan of D/s play etc but this was just nice stuff and nothing to worry about or maybe too nice if you want more heavy kink and harder "playing". <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>***********************************************************<br><br>I cross my fingers and hope the next two books (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17562579.Knight_s_Game__All_Or_Nothing___2_" title="Knight's Game (All Or Nothing, #2) by C.C. Gibbs" rel="nofollow noopener">Knight's Game</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21793847.Knight_Takes_Queen__All_Or_Nothing___3_" title="Knight Takes Queen (All Or Nothing, #3) by C.C. Gibbs" rel="nofollow noopener">Knight Takes Queen</a>) will <b>be heavier in the romantic part</b>. It is still difficult to believe in much more emotions than lust, horniness, hardness, and curiosity for the new unknown and kinky. <br><br><b>Sure it was a little romantic in the end - but not enough</b> for me. I want more red roses and love anthems.<br><blockquote>“I like Hollywood happy endings.”<br>“I thought you might.”<br>“You say it like there’s something wrong with happily ever after.”<br>“On the contrary, if only it were true the world would be a better place.”<br>“Cynic.”<br>“Welcome to my reality.”<br>“That’s what comes from making too much money.” </blockquote><br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-heart.php?page=4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396991761ra/9215448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>All in all is <i>Knight's Mistress</i> (or 'All He Wants') a good enough</b> m/f romance read. I'll pic up part two and three and finish this well done <i>All or Nothing</i> series some day. I like (need) to see that big grand HEA ending in book #3. Hopefully...<br><br>Thanks lovely SueBee for that fantastic BR you organized. ~ It was more than 1000 comments there <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1850399-epic-worldwide-buddy-read-of-all-or-nothing-book-1-on-june-11th?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">(BR thread)</a>. I think I'm the last girl who reach the finish line. ~ Better late than never!<br><br><b>I LIKE - who can resist a spoiled charmer? Not this lady.</b><br><br><br>*********************<br><br><i>The <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/101266-all-or-nothing" rel="nofollow noopener">'All or Nothing'</a> series in three novel parts by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6578577.C_C__Gibbs" title="C.C. Gibbs" rel="nofollow noopener">C.C. Gibbs</a> (aka <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/39376.Susan_Johnson" title="Susan Johnson" rel="nofollow noopener">Susan Johnson</a>).</i><br><br>UK: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17054826.Knight_s_Mistress__All_or_Nothing___1_" title="Knight's Mistress (All or Nothing, #1) by C.C. Gibbs" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1362671216s/17054826.jpg" alt="Knight's Mistress (All or Nothing, #1) by C.C. Gibbs" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18112563.Knight_s_Game__All_or_Nothing__2_" title="Knight's Game (All or Nothing #2) by C.C. Gibbs" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1372020445s/18112563.jpg" alt="Knight's Game (All or Nothing #2) by C.C. Gibbs" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18051532.Knight_Takes_Queen__All_Or_Nothing___3_" title="Knight Takes Queen (All Or Nothing, #3) by C.C. Gibbs" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1372079956s/18051532.jpg" alt="Knight Takes Queen (All Or Nothing, #3) by C.C. Gibbs" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> &amp; US: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17383702.All_He_Wants__All_Or_Nothing___1_" title="All He Wants (All Or Nothing, #1) by C.C. Gibbs" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer964626183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9813112088715671302">I was really curious as to what the Hype was all about when it came to Mr. Dominick Knight...I mean haven't we all read rich dominant alpha men who don't take no for an answer? Haven't we all read smokin' sex with pure power and submission? Haven't we all read the tale of bad boy falls for good girl before? What makes this so different? <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402674753i/9970402.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Yep, that is exactly how I felt when C.C. Gibbs threw Dominick Knight in my face. And for once...a female lead who is every bit as powerful as the man who wants </span>
  <span id="freeText9813112088715671302" style="display:none">I was really curious as to what the Hype was all about when it came to Mr. Dominick Knight...I mean haven't we all read rich dominant alpha men who don't take no for an answer? Haven't we all read smokin' sex with pure power and submission? Haven't we all read the tale of bad boy falls for good girl before? What makes this so different? <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402674753i/9970402.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yep, that is exactly how I felt when C.C. Gibbs threw Dominick Knight in my face. And for once...a female lead who is every bit as powerful as the man who wants her.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402674753i/9970403._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Katherine may not be rich or worldly, but damn if she isn't smart, sassy, and in complete ownership of what she wants. I will say I have never read of someone who could get off that much...wow, kudos to her young libido, or to him for his expertise, lol<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402674753ra/9970404.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Passion, Desire, and pure knock you on your ass emotions are what Dominick and Kate bring to the table. Unlike FSOG or Bared to You...I felt that this man was the epitome of what a true alpha should be...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402674753i/9970405._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Controlling beyond the norm, manipulative in every aspect of life to get what he wants, the mouth to piss you off yet set your panties on fire...a fine line between confident and pure asshole. He elicited love and hate from Kate and I too was struggling to come to grips with him. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402674753i/9970406.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It seems like there would be no stopping Mr.Knight on his mission to bed Kate...nothing would stop him. It was quite a feat to create a character and a story that made me question everything...made me dislike a man, yet want more of him with every page. This was filthy good love and libido chess matches...cannot wait for the outcome!</span>

<div id="review_773043313" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/773043313" />
    <a title="Angie **loves angst**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3069040-angie-loves-angst"><img alt="Angie **loves angst**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438103550p2/3069040.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/773043313?book_show_action=true">Nov 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie **loves angst**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie **loves angst**" href="/user/show/3069040-angie-loves-angst">Angie **loves angst**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer773043313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17706764875863489984"><blockquote>
<b>"He was too perfect, she wanted him too much, it was madness."</b> </blockquote><br/>I have to say that <b>Dominic Knight is everything Christian Grey wishes he could be.</b> When I read an erotica book for the first time years ago it written by Susan Johnson, and I have loved her work ever since. Now that I look back I realize that since I started reading ebooks I haven't read anything written by her so as soon as I say my dear friend Wendy reading and raving about this book I just had to read it.<br/><br/>If you enjoy reading abou</span>
  <span id="freeText17706764875863489984" style="display:none"><blockquote>
<b>"He was too perfect, she wanted him too much, it was madness."</b> </blockquote><br>I have to say that <b>Dominic Knight is everything Christian Grey wishes he could be.</b> When I read an erotica book for the first time years ago it written by Susan Johnson, and I have loved her work ever since. Now that I look back I realize that since I started reading ebooks I haven't read anything written by her so as soon as I say my dear friend Wendy reading and raving about this book I just had to read it.<br><br>If you enjoy reading about a rich, alpha, sexy, multi talented billionaire and a smart, cute, fiesty young girl with a deep sexual attraction to each other this book is for you. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385586900i/7180073.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><blockquote>
<b>"You're my dangerous unknown, my high-risk rush, my obsession."</b> </blockquote><br>When Katherine attends a job interview she meets her new boss Mr. Dominic Knight, a playboy and millionaire. She's done her research and she is aware of some of his proclivities and tastes in business and pleasure. Katherine dislikes Dominic's attitude and decides she no longer wants the job. She also has six other job offers on the table since she's very smart and fresh out of college. Dominic refuses to take no for an answer, and before she knows it, she's signing a contract and she becomes an employee of Knight Enterprises.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385587872i/7180381.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><blockquote>
  <b>"You'll like what I'm going to do to you."</b>
</blockquote><br>For me, there was a pervading sense of sadness while reading this, and even though it is low on angst and there is no crazy drama I enjoyed seeing the relationship blossom between these two. Even though Katherine is only twenty-two years old she is quite mature and smart for her age. There is no stumbling at Dominic's feet, or cowering when he's around. She stands up to him and is able verbally spar with him, not taking any of his bullshit. What I enjoyed the most is the back and forth verbal dialogue between these two. Since Katherine is very argumentative, and Mr. Knight is domineering, these two but heads many times, but in a sexy, flirty way. <br><blockquote>
<b>"You're the kind of man who might leave scars."</b> </blockquote><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385590063i/7181063._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Dominic carries a burden that causes him to be emotionally unavailable and consumed with pain. When he meets Katherine, she surprises him, because of the unexpected and unwanted emotions and feelings she stirs deep in him. He is unable to grasp why he is so addicted to her. He's puzzled as to why all of a sudden he finds himself abandoning his business just to spend time with her. He cannot understand the hold she seems to have on him, and even though he doesn't admit it, readers can tell he's scared of the emotional upheaval Katherine brings to his life.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"He didn't believe in magic, but if he did, he would have found her magical. A sweet escape from the cynicism of his life."</b>
</blockquote><br>Susan Johnson's writing is even better than ever. The words and phrases she uses evoked so many emotions, I felt the turmoil within these characters. The last five percent was achingly beautiful and left me with high anticipation for Book two. I look forward to seeing where SJ takes this couple and their journey to a HEA.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385588666i/7180596.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
<b> "Its frightening to be this obsessed."</b> </blockquote><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>"And all the time he'd been making love, he'd been leaving her."</b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Rating: 5 I Loved It From The First Line Stars.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15940962805498074760">First of all - thank you for the signed copy! Won via Goodreads First Reads. This book is real.<br/><br/>Knight's Mistress is set over a few short days, but just like falling in love those few short days seem to</span>
  <span id="freeText15940962805498074760" style="display:none">First of all - thank you for the signed copy! Won via Goodreads First Reads. This has in no way altered my judgement of this book and my review is honest.<br /><br />I thought Knight's Mistress was going to be just another 50-Shades-esque book. The beginning was deja-vu - intimidating-billionaire-interview, instant-attraction and inner monologues. But it's not. This book is different. This book is real.<br /><br />Knight's Mistress is set over a few short days, but just like falling in love those few short days seem to last forever. And that makes this book, no matter how unrealistic the circumstances, completely believeable.<br /><br />Katherine is a strong character, a no-nonsense young woman who knows what she wants and will get it. She's strong, with her own opinions, and she's SMART. She's very smart.<br /><br />Dominic is your typical more-money-than-sense but he still cares. He was never going to force Katherine into anything she didn't want.<br /><br />Both characters are devastatingly manipulative with each other, but they both know it and it's like a game. The balance between the characters is excellent. It focuses mostly on Kate, but when Dominic gets his narrative voice it sets them on equal footing and strengthens them both as characters.<br /><br />I didn't like the constant "Ummmm". Ummmm to me is an indecisive noise, the sound you make when you're not sure what to say. I'd have preferred some Hmmm and Mmmm and Ahhh to break it up a little, and "Ummmm" did distract from my reading a little.<br /><br />And Katherine must be EXHAUSTED. Every single muscle in her body tensing and un-tensing in such quick succession, over and over? It's dangerous to be that sensitive!<br /><br />The ending was not what I expected, but I was glad for the twist. Although not a major cliffhanger, I'd happily read on in this series, if only to see if things will get better. They have to, right?<br /><br />I think I'll go drink some chocolate milk now. Or some coffee. I'm not a fan of either, but this book has put the notion in my head.<br /><br /><i>I received a copy of this for free via Goodreads First Reads.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="15940962805498074760" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yvQ/bZUvudGXqw6kGyirvYmxUuxr1uhq4lTF+krij3JdWsuf6u5bcq8wCWbw1OhglRuxVR0qSxobGPu+F6701A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KJCGo6Te5jTx8u3Pw/2MueTY4ro7Pz4ZYl6SAEgPahG/PnJR2x8El8lp6g0oAc9k+HIBA03DnWmbEqxEFUMRtw==')})
  }
